You can separate strings by comma. Each valid string must be of at least 4 and no more than 25 symbols. Do not specify a very common strings like 'beta', 'menu', 'free', etc because these are natural words that might be present in games even without mods. If you specify an important string, that was present inside process before launching the mod, then this might lead to game crash in some cases. Please note that ExLoader treats strings as partial or full matches. This means that if your string is 'ground', then any word that contains this sequence will be erased ('battleground', 'playground', etc.). You can fix this by specifying strings of exact match and partial match into separate fields.
